## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="39a7c-1250">Atributos do Windows Server 2012</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39a7c-1250">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="39a7c-1251">Essa classe contém os seguintes atributos para o Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="39a7c-1251">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
